[16/11/18, 8:57:13â€¯AM] Samir Arora-President- NAR ğŸ‡®ğŸ‡³: ğŸ™
[16/11/18, 9:35:43â€¯AM] Samir Arora-President- NAR ğŸ‡®ğŸ‡³: Ladies and Gentlemen
There has been some amount of communication on Nobroker.com and other companies that are working on newer Disruptive models of business in Real Estate. The CREA (I) Committee met up to take an overview of the situation and here are a few observations for all our Members.

1. Disruption is the name of the game now in almost all industries and more so in Real Estate post RERA.
2. We need to focus on growing our business but we cannot stop any Business model, just because it disrupts a traditional norm and challenges the past. FYI, OYO from Hotels is moving to Real Estate too and Funded companies will bring more innovations and disruptions in next 2/3 years in India than we have seen in last 70 years in Real Estate.
3. Fighting Nobroker.com for advertising and pulling down brokers on visual ads may be justifiable. But we cannot stop a company from not charging a owner or a financial model of their business plan. Let us be clear on that.
4. Some Realtors charge Owners less than one month Rent in Residential complexes and some do not charge the owner. Are they any different from No Broker except that they are not funded or large? I think it's time to check ourselves first.
5. CREA (I) has been very protective and will continue to be so for all its Members. However in recent times Members have not supported the cause for themselves fully in many counts.
Prima facie,

A/  Vaishnavi Serene
Launch at Taj West End is attended by 350 people. On site Visit and Meet organised by Committee is confirmed by 90 members and attended by 20. Just 20. The Committee for all its work has reasons to feel Let Down by the Members here. We still have time to change that perception by more involvement by Members.

B/ A simple Google Form that takes 2 minutes of your time for Profiling our members has been filled only by 40 out of 300 members till date. The Committee is unable to research and offer Tailor made solutions to Developers for your Business growth without that data. If we cannot give 2 min as Members then I think it's Time to realize that a dozen people at Committee are investing too much time, effort and energy fighting every cause for our Realtor Members.

C/ The last Training drew fantabulous reviews. But a subsidized Training also draws only 75/80 members from 300. If we are not even willing to learn, educate ourselves and progress together, then we are not there yet to fight Disruptive companies and Market evolutions.

It is Time to Reflect, Regroup and Reorganize ourselves and Members involvement and participation is what will decide the future course of CREA (I) events and directions.
We have been the most pro active association for years now and we can see that confidently PAN India with our interactions. However, there are associations in different cities that are progressing phenomenally and like in our business, if we do not adapt and act to the changing times quickly, we will not remain the Best.
Do we want to remain the No 1 is the question? Yes, obviously is the answer. Can the Committee do it without Members? No is the only answer.
Are the Members willing to change and promise/commit to participate proactively?
We will wait for that answer.
Thankyou ğŸ™
On Behalf of CREA (I) Committee

General Secretary.
